exec sp_executesql N'SELECT 
	a.record_id, a.appointment_id, a.appointment_number, a.owner_type, a.owner_id, a.organizer_id, a.creator_id, a.private, a.app_date, a.appt_flags, a.end_date, a.textcol, CASE WHEN a.owner_type = 101 THEN a.textcol ELSE r.name END AS owner_name, a.rsvp, a.alert_flag, a.lead_date, a.snooze_end_date, ab.client_id, ab.contact_number, ab.name_type, ab.record_type, ab.company_name, ab.first_name, ab.initial, ab.last_name, a.client_id, a.contact_number, ld.lead_id, ld.lead_number, ld.company, ld.first_name, ld.last_name, ld.middle_name, a.lead_id, a.lead_number, a.recurring_id
FROM 
	amgr_appointments_tbl a
	LEFT JOIN amgr_resources r ON r.resource_id = a.owner_id AND r.record_type = (1 + a.owner_type) AND a.owner_type IN (0, 1, 2)
	LEFT JOIN (
SELECT 
	amgr_client_tbl.client_id, amgr_client_tbl.contact_number, amgr_client_tbl.name_type, amgr_client_tbl.record_type, CASE WHEN company.record_type IN (''2'') THEN company.firm WHEN company.record_type IN (''5'') THEN '''' ELSE company.name END AS company_name, amgr_client_tbl.first_name, amgr_client_tbl.initial, CASE WHEN amgr_client_tbl.record_type IN (''1'',''5'') THEN '''' ELSE amgr_client_tbl.name END AS last_name
FROM 
	amgr_client_tbl
	JOIN amgr_client_tbl company ON company.client_id = amgr_client_tbl.client_id AND company.contact_number = 0
) ab ON ab.client_id = a.client_id AND ab.contact_number = a.contact_number
	LEFT JOIN (
SELECT 
	lead_tbl.lead_id, lead_tbl.lead_number, lead_tbl.company, lead_tbl.first_name, lead_tbl.last_name, lead_tbl.middle_name
FROM 
	lead_tbl
) ld ON a.lead_id = ld.lead_id AND a.lead_number = ld.lead_number
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT 
	t.appointment_id, t.appointment_number
FROM 
	amgr_appointments_tbl t
WHERE 
((t.owner_id = @UID0 AND COALESCE(t.owner_type, 0) = 0) AND (t.completed = @B1 OR t.completed IS NULL) AND (t.rsvp <> @I2 OR t.rsvp IS NULL) AND (t.alert_flag = @I3 OR (t.alert_flag = @I4 AND t.lead_date BETWEEN @D5 AND @D6 AND (t.snooze_end_date <= @D7 OR t.snooze_end_date IS NULL))))
) s ON s.appointment_id = a.appointment_id AND s.appointment_number = a.appointment_number
ORDER BY 
	a.appointment_id ASC, a.appointment_number ASC 
',N'@UID0 nvarchar(10),@B1 smallint,@I2 smallint,@I3 smallint,@I4 smallint,@D5 datetime,@D6 datetime,@D7 datetime',@UID0=N'MARMSTRONG',@B1=0,@I2=2,@I3=2,@I4=1,@D5='2024-07-30 21:04:20',@D6='2024-08-13 21:04:20',@D7='2024-08-13 21:04:20'

exec sp_executesql N'SELECT 
	t.task_id, t.task_number, t.start_date, t.task_flags, t.description, t.owner_id, t.completed, t.snooze_end_date, ab.client_id, ab.contact_number, ab.name_type, ab.record_type, ab.company_name, ab.first_name, ab.initial, ab.last_name, t.parent_id, t.parent_number, t.parent_type, rc.record_id, ld.lead_id, ld.lead_number, ld.company, ld.first_name, ld.last_name, ld.middle_name
FROM 
	task_tbl t
	LEFT JOIN (
SELECT 
	amgr_client_tbl.client_id, amgr_client_tbl.contact_number, amgr_client_tbl.name_type, amgr_client_tbl.record_type, CASE WHEN company.record_type IN (''2'') THEN company.firm WHEN company.record_type IN (''5'') THEN '''' ELSE company.name END AS company_name, amgr_client_tbl.first_name, amgr_client_tbl.initial, CASE WHEN amgr_client_tbl.record_type IN (''1'',''5'') THEN '''' ELSE amgr_client_tbl.name END AS last_name
FROM 
	amgr_client_tbl
	JOIN amgr_client_tbl company ON company.client_id = amgr_client_tbl.client_id AND company.contact_number = 0
) ab ON t.parent_type = 1 AND ab.client_id = t.parent_id AND ab.contact_number = t.parent_number
	LEFT JOIN task_recurrence_tbl rc ON rc.record_id = t.recurring_id
	LEFT JOIN (
SELECT 
	lead_tbl.lead_id, lead_tbl.lead_number, lead_tbl.company, lead_tbl.first_name, lead_tbl.last_name, lead_tbl.middle_name
FROM 
	lead_tbl
) ld ON t.parent_type = 19 AND t.parent_id = ld.lead_id AND t.parent_number = ld.lead_number
WHERE 
((t.owner_id = @UID0 AND (t.completed = @B1 OR t.completed IS NULL) AND t.alarm > 0 AND t.lead_date BETWEEN @D2 AND @D3 AND (t.snooze_end_date <= @D4 OR t.snooze_end_date IS NULL)) AND t.entry_type != 4 AND 
            (
		        t.owner_id = @CURRENTUID5
		        OR 
		        EXISTS(	
			        SELECT 
				        1 
			        FROM
				        admn_users u 
				        INNER JOIN admn_users1 u1 ON u.record_id = u1.record_id 
			        WHERE 
				        u.user_id = t.owner_id
                        AND
                        1 = 1
                        AND 
				        (
					        ''*'' IN (u1.hotlistuserbusy, u1.hotlistusermodify) 
					        OR 
					        @CURRENTUID5 IN (u1.hotlistuserbusy, u1.hotlistusermodify) 
					        OR 
					        EXISTS(

            SELECT   
                t.data_machine_id, t.sequence_number, 1, t.type_id, t.code_id, t.tag, t.maxmerge_lock, t.style_id, t.hotlist, t.def_type, t.client_type, t.priv, t.owner_id, t.record_id, t.creator_id, t.create_date, t.readpriv, t.readonly_id, t.mandatory, t.requestor_id, t.customsort, t.inactive, 
                CASE 
                    WHEN t.code_id = 0 THEN t.description 
                    WHEN name1.code_id = 0 THEN name1.description + ''\'' + t.description
                    WHEN name2.code_id = 0 THEN name2.description + ''\'' + name1.description + ''\'' + t.description
                    ELSE name3.description + ''\'' + name2.description + ''\'' + name1.description + ''\'' + t.description
                END AS path, des.description
            FROM 
                amgr_user_field_defs_tbl AS t
                LEFT OUTER JOIN amgr_user_field_defs_tbl AS name1 ON t.code_id = name1.type_id AND name1.table_id = 1 
                LEFT OUTER JOIN amgr_user_field_defs_tbl AS name2 ON name1.code_id = name2.type_id AND name2.table_id = 1
                LEFT OUTER JOIN amgr_user_field_defs_tbl AS name3 ON name2.code_id = name3.type_id AND name3.table_id = 1
                LEFT OUTER JOIN amgr_descriptions AS des ON des.rec_machine_id = t.data_machine_id AND t.sequence_number = des.rec_seq_number AND des.record_type = 3

dbo.ADMN_User_Details.User_Id = dbo.ADMN_Users.User_Id LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.AMGR_Resources ON dbo.AMGR_Resources.Resource_Id = dbo.ADMN_Users.User_Id AND dbo.AMGR_Resources.Record_Type = 1 WHERE dbo.ADMN_Users.User_Id = 0x54004800550043004B00

--...
